Map/Summary/PAiur01=光复艾尔的行动开始了。在控制了时空航道之后，黄金舰队已能在行星的空中地带自由驰骋。但在发现一支野生异虫部队受到了一名混合体的控制之后，阿塔尼斯开始深思起泽拉图对战争的警告。 /// The reclamation of Aiur has begun. With the warp conduits secured, the Golden Armada now sweeps across the planet's skies. But the discovery of a hybrid commanding the once feral zerg broods leaves Artanis troubled over Zeratul's warnings of the war to come.
Map/Summary/PAiur02=泽拉图死了，他为了切断阿塔尼斯的神经束，倒在了埃蒙的刀下。但是年轻的大主教并没有多少时间去为故人悲痛，还有更为重要的使命等待着他去完成。卡拉遭到了腐化，所有与之相连的星灵都屈从于埃蒙的意志。阿塔尼斯集结起仅存的部队，准备效仿黑暗圣堂武士那样，去解救更多的同胞。 /// Zeratul is dead, slain by Amon while severing Artanis's nerve cords. But the young Hierarch has much to do before he can grieve for his fallen friend. The Khala is corrupted, binding all those within it to Amon's will. Artanis rallies his remaining forces as the last of the Dark Templar work to free more of their brethren.
Map/Summary/PAiur03=艾尔落入了埃蒙之手。幸存的圣堂武士逃离了母星并登上了亚顿之矛，侥幸从埃蒙手中逃脱……但只是暂时脱险而已。在没有了卡拉和黄金舰队之后，阿塔尼斯必须团结起新朋故友，才能在接下来的日子里再一次面对黑暗之神。 /// Aiur has fallen to Amon. The surviving Templar flee from their home world aboard the Spear of Adun, narrowly escaping Amon's grasp... for now. Without the Khala or the Golden Armada, Artanis must call upon allies old and new before confronting the Dark One again.
Map/Summary/PAiur04=真正能终结埃蒙的机会出现了。阿塔尼斯和他的盟友在整个艾尔星球上齐心协力，成功摧毁了这颗星球的折跃网络，阻止了黄金舰队的回归。但他们只是暂时拖延了无敌舰队的抵达时间而已，必须抓住这个机会消灭埃蒙的宿体。 /// The time has come to end Amon once and for all. Working together across all of Aiur, Artanis and his allies have destroyed the planet's warp network and prevented the return of the Golden Armada. But they have only delayed the Great Fleet's arrival, and must use the time they have left to eliminate Amon's host body.
Map/Summary/PAiur05=经过一番苦战之后，阿塔尼斯和他的盟友赶在埃蒙的宿体复活的那一刻成功将其摧毁。但他们必须将埃蒙囚禁在钥石内足够长的时间，以便让剩余的圣堂武士有机会切断自身与卡拉的连接。最终之战即将到来，而埃蒙必将为之倾其所有。只有团结一心才能取得最终的胜利。 /// After a hard fought battle, Artanis and his allies destroyed Amon's host body just as it came to life. But they must still imprison Amon within the Keystone long enough for the rest of the Templar to sever themselves from the Khala. The final confrontation lies ahead, and Amon will bring all of his might down upon them. Only in unity can they prevail.
Map/Summary/PAiur06=埃蒙被打败了，并被逐回了虚空。尽管卡拉已不复存在，等待着星灵的却是一个崭新的黄金纪元。感谢所有英勇献身的战士和英雄，让和平的曙光再次出现在地平线上。但要真正消灭埃蒙，还有一项终极挑战需要面对。<n/><n/>进入虚空，在《星际争霸II》三部曲的最终章中体验这部史诗科幻大剧的大结局。 /// Amon has been defeated and banished back into the Void. Though the Khala is no more, the protoss stand on the cusp of a new golden age. Thanks to the efforts and sacrifices of brave warriors and heroes, peace can once again be glimpsed upon the horizon. But one final task remains if Amon is to be truly destroyed.<n/><n/>Experience the epic conclusion with Into the Void, the final chapter in the StarCraft II trilogy.
Map/Summary/PKorhal01=在阿塔尼斯和雷诺的共同努力下，天空之盾坠向克哈大气层的灾难性危机得到了消解。在消除了莫比斯军团的威胁之后，阿塔尼斯准备重提此次前来帝国星域的要事：取得钥石并追寻泽拉图的预言指引。 /// Sky Shield's catastrophic descent into Korhal's atmosphere has been prevented, thanks to the combined efforts of Artanis and Raynor. With the threat of Moebius Corps forestalled, Artanis turns his attention to the reason for his journey into Dominion space: acquiring the Keystone and pursuing Zeratul's prophecies.
Map/Summary/PKorhal02=钥石到手了，但是人类却为此承受了巨大的伤亡。即便是现在，埃蒙的部队仍在席卷帝国的疆域，散布着死亡与毁灭。雷诺和阿塔尼斯现今各自分路，双方都下定决心要拼死挽救自己的人民。 /// The Keystone has been secured, though the terrans have suffered enormous casualties in the process. Even now, Amon's forces cut a swath through Dominion space, leaving death and destruction in their wake. Raynor and Artanis now go their separate ways, each of them determined to fight for the survival of their people.
Map/Summary/PMoebius01=在阿塔尼斯的勇士们拼死保卫亚顿之矛期间，凯拉克斯力排万难，成功摧毁了埃蒙最后一处混合体培育设施。尽管这位卡莱阶层出身的相位技师缺乏战斗训练，但他达成的这项英勇壮举，足以让他配得上最勇敢的圣堂武士的称号。 /// While Artanis's warriors defended the Spear of Adun, Karax defied all odds and successfully  destroyed Amon's last remaining hybrid breeding facility. Despite his lack of combat training, the Khalai phase-smith has accomplished a feat of heroism worthy of the bravest of Templar.
Map/Summary/PPurifier01=在有了阿拉纳克以及塔达林一族的帮助之后，阿塔尼斯还从格拉修斯的一处卡莱设施中找到了一种实验性的净化者武器。凯拉克斯相信，这项全新科技将在对抗埃蒙的战争中发挥出巨大作用。 /// Despite the efforts of Alarak and the Tal'darim, Artanis has retrieved a cache of experimental Purifier weaponry from a Khalai facility on Glacius. Karax is confident that this new technology will prove invaluable in the war against Amon.
Map/Summary/PPurifier02=阿塔尼斯的部队在艾迪昂星球上的异虫感染区中杀出了一条血路，并将塞布罗斯号从几个世纪的静滞状态中唤醒。现在，这艘船上的古老净化者们即将再次苏醒。虽然它们对神之长子充满了敌意，不过阿塔尼斯认为自己能说服它们加入对抗埃蒙的战争。 /// Artanis's forces have cleared a path through the zerg infestation on Endion and released Cybros from its centuries in stasis. Now the ancient Purifiers aboard the warship can be reawakened. Despite their hostility toward the Firstborn, Artanis is confident he can secure their support in the war against Amon.
Map/Summary/PPurifier03=净化者们再一次醒来。在执行官科罗拉里昂的指挥下，它们净化了塞布罗斯号上的异虫，并将其视为自己的家园而重新夺回。它们完全可以成为有力的盟友……但首先，阿塔尼斯必须化解历史隔阂，并说服它们放下对自己的星灵创造者们由来已久的敌意。 /// The Purifiers are awake once again. Under the command of Executor Clolarion, they have cleansed Cybros of the zerg and reclaimed it as their home. They could prove to be powerful allies... but first, Artanis must make amends for the past and convince them to set aside their age-old enmity toward their protoss creators.
Map/Summary/PShakuras01=萨古拉斯遭到了埃蒙的混合体以及异虫的蹂躏，无数的奈拉齐姆在这场攻击中丧命。那些幸存的星灵已经撤离了这颗星球的地表，现在已追随族长沃拉尊，与阿塔尼斯并肩作战。虽然黑暗圣堂武士成为了强力的盟友，但是在埃蒙无情的攻势下，萨古拉斯这颗星球恐怕不保。 /// Shakuras is overrun with Amon's hybrid and zerg, and countless Nerazim were slaughtered in the attack. Those that survive have been evacuated from the planet's surface and now follow Matriarch Vorazun alongside Artanis. The Dark Templar make for strong allies, but Shakuras may be lost to Amon's unrelenting advance.
Map/Summary/PShakuras02=萨古拉斯不复存在了，在一场巨大的爆炸中化为了虚无，这一切都是为了防止埃蒙将这颗星球据为己有。如今的星灵一族已无处为家，成为了一群漂泊在亚顿之矛上的流浪者，苦苦寻觅着反击仇敌的机会。 /// Shakuras is no more, obliterated in a massive explosion to prevent Amon from seizing the planet as his own. The protoss now stand without a home, a vagabond people aboard the Spear of Adun, seeking a way to strike back at their great enemy.
Map/Summary/PTaldarim01=作为双方停火的交换，阿塔尼斯同意协助阿拉纳克夺取塔达林的领导权。在阿拉纳克的坚持下，阿塔尼斯消灭了高阶领主马拉什的守护者……结果却发现自己被利用了，这场战斗与仪式根本毫无关系。 /// In exchange for a ceasefire between their people, Artanis has agreed to aid Alarak in usurping the leadership of the Tal'darim. At Alarak's insistence, Artanis eliminated Highlord Ma'lash's guardians... only to learn that he had been deceived, and that the battle had nothing to do with the ritual.
Map/Summary/PTaldarim02=阿拉纳克除掉了马拉什，夺取了塔达林的统治权。所有塔达林如今对埃蒙倒戈相向，他们已不再是阿塔尼斯部队的威胁。不过，如果阿塔尼斯能说服阿拉纳克和他并肩战斗的话，那可真是如虎添翼了。 /// Alarak has slain Ma'lash and seized control of the Tal'darim.  They now turn against Amon and no longer present a threat to Artanis's forces. If he can convince Alarak to fight alongside him, however, Artanis stands to gain a powerful new ally.
Map/Summary/PUlnar01=在钥石的指引下，亚顿之矛现在来到了乌尔纳的轨道上空，也就是传说中的萨尔纳加的家园。阿塔尼斯从塔达林手上夺取了神庙，并打开了进入下方大厅中的入口。兑现泽拉图最终预言的时刻到来了。 /// Led by the Keystone, the Spear of Adun now orbits Ulnar, fabled home of the xel'naga. Artanis has secured the temple from the Tal'darim and unsealed the entrance into the halls below. The time to fulfill Zeratul's final prophecy has come to pass.
Map/Summary/PUlnar02=阿塔尼斯与刀锋女王一同发现了萨尔纳加一族的宏伟意图，并进入了他们沉睡的大厅。但是他来迟了。埃蒙已经杀死了所有的萨尔纳加，现在正准备进入一个他自己创造的宿体之中。泽拉图预示的希望似乎破灭了，但阿坦尼斯依然对这最后一丝光明坚信不移。 /// Alongside the Queen of Blades, Artanis has uncovered the great purpose of the xel'naga and entered the chamber wherein they slumber. But he is too late. Amon has killed his brethren and is now poised to enter a host body of his own creation. The hope heralded by Zeratul seems lost, but Artanis stands firm against the dying light.
Map/Summary/PUlnar03=由于对埃蒙背弃塔达林一事心怀怨恨，阿拉纳克将阿塔尼斯陷入危险一事告诉了沃拉尊。在非常不情愿地接受他的帮助后，沃拉尊带领亚顿之矛上的圣堂武士展开了一场营救大主教的冒险行动。没有了泽拉图预言的指引，星灵如今必须自行制定今后的行动计划。 /// Incensed by Amon's betrayal of the Tal'darim, Alarak warns Vorazun that Artanis is in danger. After reluctantly accepting his help, Vorazun leads the Templar aboard the Spear of Adun in a daring rescue of their Hierarch. Without Zeratul's prophecies to guide them, the protoss must now chart a new course of action on their own.
Map/Summary/SC2Epilogue01=凯瑞甘，雷诺和阿塔尼斯率领各自的部队远征虚空，准备一劳永逸地终结埃蒙。战斗虽然很艰苦，但他们成功杀死了纳鲁德并在这个黑暗的位面中建立起了一处落脚点。现在，他们正寻觅着一个神秘而又慈善的声音的源头，这个声音一直以来呼唤着他们。 /// Kerrigan, Raynor and Artanis lead their forces on an expedition into the Void to end Amon once and for all. The battle has been difficult, but their armies have nonetheless succeeded in killing Narud and establishing a foothold within this dark realm. Now they seek the source of the mysterious yet benevolent voice that called them to action.
Map/Summary/SC2Epilogue02=凯瑞甘拥抱自己命运的时刻到来了。在雷诺和阿塔尼斯的帮助下，她吸收了最后一任萨尔纳加——奥鲁斯的精华。继承了强大的力量后，她已经准备好要永远地终结埃蒙。 /// The time has come for Kerrigan to embrace her destiny. With the help of Raynor and Artanis, she has absorbed the essence of Ouros, last of the xel'naga. With the awesome power she has inherited, she stands ready to end Amon once and for all.
Map/Summary/SC2Epilogue03=终于，埃蒙灭亡了。凯瑞甘成为了萨尔纳加，为无尽的轮回划下了句点。科普卢星区的居民们如今致力于重建与恢复，使凯瑞甘英勇的牺牲不致白费。<n/><n/>帝国起起落落、星球成住坏空，神灵亦死亦生。在这波澜壮阔的历史长河中，无数勇敢的指挥官们率领他们的部队走向了胜利，为自己的人民争取到了自由与和平。《星际争霸II》的史诗篇章就此落幕。感谢您成就了这段传奇。 /// At long last, Amon is no more. Kerrigan has become xel'naga and ended the Infinite Cycle. The denizens of the Koprulu sector now focus on reconstruction and recovery, making the most of Kerrigan's valiant sacrifice.<n/><n/>Empires have fallen, worlds have been shattered, and gods have been slain. Through it all, brave commanders have led their forces to victory and secured peace and freedom for their people. The saga of StarCraft II has ended. Thank you for playing.
